import CaptionText from '/src/components/CaptionText.astro';

The following information refers to symbols present in _Handbook of the International Phonetic Association_, (Cambridge: Cambridge University Press, 1999), pp. 164-184.

#### Unicode characters

The following table shows the Unicode characters that have equivalent IPA symbols.

Note 1: It is preferable to use precomposed characters with the tilde and hooks as found in the Phonetic Extensions block or IPA Extensions block.

#### Unicode character sequences

The following symbols correspond to a sequence of Unicode characters.

| IPA Number | IPA Name | Graphics | USVs | IPA Description | Status |
| ---------- | -------- | -------- | ---- | --------------- | ------ |
| 529 | Rising tone letter | :usv[02E9]{char}:usv[02E5]{char} | [02E9](/char/U0002E9) [02E5](/char/U0002E5) | Rising contour |  |
| 530 | Falling tone letter | :usv[02E5]{char}:usv[02E9]{char} | [02E5](/char/U0002E5) [02E9](/char/U0002E9) | Falling contour |  |
| 531 | High-rising tone letter | :usv[02E7]{char}:usv[02E5]{char} | [02E7](/char/U0002E7) [02E5](/char/U0002E5) | High rising contour |  |
| 532 | Low-rising tone letter | :usv[02E9]{char}:usv[02E7]{char} | [02E9](/char/U0002E9) [02E7](/char/U0002E7) | Low rising contour |  |
| 533 | Rising-falling tone letter | :usv[02E8]{char}:usv[02E5]{char}:usv[02E8]{char} | [02E8](/char/U0002E8) [02E5](/char/U0002E5) [02E8](/char/U0002E8) | Rising-falling contour |  |
| 631 | Bracketed single period | :usv[0028]{char}:usv[002E]{char}:usv[0029]{char} | [0028](/char/U000028) [002E](/char/U00002E) [0029](/char/U000029) | Short pause | (use 506) |
| 632 | Bracketed double period | :usv[0028]{char}:usv[002E]{char}:usv[002E]{char}:usv[0029]{char} | [0028](/char/U000028) [002E](/char/U00002E) [002E](/char/U00002E) [0029](/char/U000029) | Medium-length pause | (use 506) |
| 633 | Bracketed triple period | :usv[0028]{char}:usv[002E]{char}:usv[002E]{char}:usv[002E]{char}:usv[0029]{char} | [0028](/char/U000028) [002E](/char/U00002E) [002E](/char/U00002E) [002E](/char/U00002E) [0029](/char/U000029) | Long pause | (use 506) |
| 635 | Fortissimo | :usv[1D191]{char}:usv[1D191]{char} | [1D191](/char/U001D191) [1D191](/char/U001D191) | Louder speech |  |
| 637 | Pianissimo | :usv[1D18F]{char}:usv[1D18F]{char} | [1D18F](/char/U001D18F) [1D18F](/char/U001D18F) | Quieter speech |  |
| 653 | Superscript+subscript bridge | :usv[032A]{char}:usv[0346]{char} | [032A](/char/U00032A) [0346](/char/U000346) | Bidental articulation |  |
| 665 | Bracketed subscript wedge | :usv[208D]{char}:usv[02EC]{char}:usv[208E]{char} | [208D](/char/U00208D) [02EC](/char/U0002EC) [208E](/char/U00208E) | Partial voicing |  |
| 666 | Left-bracketed subscript wedge | :usv[208D]{char}:usv[02EC]{char} | [208D](/char/U00208D) [02EC](/char/U0002EC) | Initial partial voicing |  |
| 667 | Right-bracketed subscript wedge | :usv[02EC]{char}:usv[208E]{char} | [02EC](/char/U0002EC) [208E](/char/U00208E) | Final partial voicing |  |
| 668 | Bracketed under-ring | :usv[208D]{char}:usv[02F3]{char}:usv[208E]{char} | [208D](/char/U00208D) [02F3](/char/U0002F3) [208E](/char/U00208E) | Partial devoicing |  |
| 669 | Left-bracketed under-ring | :usv[208D]{char}:usv[02F3]{char} | [208D](/char/U00208D) [02F3](/char/U0002F3) | Initial partial devoicing |  |
| 670 | Right-bracketed under-ring | :usv[02F3]{char}:usv[208E]{char} | [02F3](/char/U0002F3) [208E](/char/U00208E) | Final partial devoicing |  |
| 672 | Right-sited double exclamation point | :usv[01C3]{char}:usv[01C3]{char} | [01C3](/char/U0001C3) [01C3](/char/U0001C3) | Ventricular |  |
| 908 | Left double parenthesis | :usv[0028]{char}:usv[0028]{char} | [0028](/char/U000028) [0028](/char/U000028) | Sound obscured (begin) |  |
| 909 | Right double parenthesis | :usv[0029]{char}:usv[0029]{char} | [0029](/char/U000029) [0029](/char/U000029) | Sound obscured (end) |  |"
